Description: 7-transmembrane G-linked receptors: list of entries
Name:        7tmrlist.txt
Release:     2017_08 of 30-Aug-2017

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Various types of information about 7-transmembrane G-linked receptors - also
known as  G-protein coupled receptors (GPCR) - can be found in the following
WWW servers:

GPCRDB:  http://www.gpcr.org/7tm/
NIH   :  http://mgddk1.niddk.nih.gov/GPCR.shtml
HORDE :  http://bip.weizmann.ac.il/HORDE/
ORDB  :  http://senselab.med.yale.edu/senselab/ORDB/default.asp
